style="text-align:center"><span><br/></span></div></div></div><div id="i980c7c1ec2b848fea488220defc0485a_7"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:42.75pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="-sec-extract:summary"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item&#160;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On April&#160;18, 2024, Netflix, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced its financial results for the quarter ended March&#160;31, 2024. The Letter to Shareholders, which is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference, includes reference to the non-GAAP financial information. A reconciliation to the GAAP equivalent of non-GAAP measures is contained in tabular form in Exhibit 99.1. We are not able to reconcile forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures because we are unable to predict without unreasonable effort the exact amount or timing of the reconciling items, including property and equipment and change in other assets, and the impact of changes in currency exchange rates. The variability of these items could have a significant impact on our future GAAP financial results. </span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:24.75pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The information contained in this Item 2.02 and the accompanying Exhibit 99.1 are &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, and shall not be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, unless expressly incorporated by specific reference in such filing.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 8.01 Other Events.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On April 12, 2024, Netflix, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) entered into a Senior Unsecured Revolving Credit Agreement (the &#8220;Revolving Credit Agreement&#8221;) among the Company, the lenders party thereto and JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., as the administrative agent. The Revolving Credit Agreement provides for a $3,000,000,000 unsecured revolving credit facility. The Company did not borrow any amount under the Revolving Credit Agreement at closing. The Company may use the proceeds of future borrowings under the Revolving Credit Agreement for working capital and general corporate purposes.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revolving loans may be borrowed, repaid and reborrowed until April 12, 2029, at which time all amounts borrowed must be repaid. Revolving loans may be prepaid without premium or penalty. </span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revolving loans will bear interest, at the Company&#8217;s option, at either (i) a floating rate per annum equal to a base rate (the &#8220;Alternate Base Rate&#8221;) plus an applicable margin or (ii) a per annum rate equal to an adjusted term SOFR rate (the &#8220;Adjusted Term SOFR Rate&#8221;) plus an applicable margin. The applicable margin for Alternate Base Rate loans will range from 0% to 0.25%, and the applicable margin for Adjusted Term SOFR Rate loans will range from 0.75% to 1.25%, each based on the Company&#8217;s credit ratings. </span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Revolving Credit Agreement contains customary affirmative covenants and negative covenants (and customary baskets and exceptions with respect thereto) for a credit facility of this size and type, including covenants that require delivery of financial statements and notices of events of default; and covenants that limit or restrict the ability of the Company and its subsidiaries to incur debt for borrowed money that is secured by liens, and limitations on the Company&#8217;s ability to merge or consolidate. The Revolving Credit Agreement also requires the Company to maintain a minimum ratio of consolidated EBITDA to consolidated interest expense of 3.0 to 1.0 as of the last day of each fiscal quarter.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Revolving Credit Agreement includes customary events of default (subject to customary grace periods), including payment defaults, inaccuracy of representations or warranties in any material respect, violation of covenants, cross acceleration to other material indebtedness, bankruptcy and insolvency events involving the Company or its significant subsidiaries, material judgments, certain ERISA events and a change of control that is accompanied with or followed by a downgrade of the debt rating of the Company that is below an investment-grade debt rating. The occurrence of an event of default could result in the termination of the lenders&#8217; commitments and the acceleration of the obligations under the Revolving Credit Agreement, if any.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt;text-indent:27pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In connection with its entry into the Revolving Credit Agreement, the Company terminated the Revolving Credit Agreement dated as of July 27, 2017, as amended, by and among the Company, Morgan Stanley Senior Funding, Inc., as administrative agent, and the lenders party thereto.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-bottom:5pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:72.618%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"><div><img alt="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" src="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" style="height:22px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:86px"></div></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">1</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><div id="ic73c69464ad74468b98bc857bf74a722_4"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Q1 Results</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">In Q1, revenue grew 15% year over year, or 18% on a foreign exchange (F&#47;X) neutral basis</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, driven primarily by membership growth as well as pricing. ARM</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> rose 1% year over year, or 4% on a F&#47;X neutral basis. The difference between F&#47;X neutral growth and our reported growth was primarily driven by the impact of price increases in Argentina due to local inflation and the 75% decrease in the </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Argentine peso</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> relative to the US dollar. Revenue was above our guidance as paid net additions (9.3M vs. 1.8M in Q1&#8217;23) were higher than we forecast. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Operating income in Q1&#8217;24 totaled $2.6B (vs. $1.7B in Q1&#8216;23) &#8212; a year over year increase of 54%. This was also above our forecast primarily due to our higher than anticipated revenue and the timing of our content spend. Operating margin of 28% grew seven percentage points year over year (vs. 21% last Q1).  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">EPS for the first quarter was $5.28 vs. $2.88 last year and our $4.49 forecast. Net income included a $131 million non-cash unrealized gain from F&#47;X remeasurement on our Euro denominated debt, which is recognized below operating income in &#8220;interest and other income.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As we noted in our last letter, our two priorities in ads are to scale our member base and to build out our capabilities for advertisers. We made progress on both fronts in Q1. Our ads membership grew 65% quarter on quarter (after rising nearly 70% sequentially in each of Q3&#8217;23 and Q4&#8217;23) with over 40% of all signups in our ads markets coming from our ads plan. For advertisers, we continue to focus on measurement solutions, including new partnerships with Kantar and Lucid for brand awareness and recall, and Nielsen Catalina Solutions for sales lift and we&#8217;re working to build out our sales capabilities.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Forecast</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As a reminder, the quarterly guidance we provide is our actual internal forecast at the time we report. Our primary financial metrics are revenue for growth and operating margin for profitability. Our goals are to sustain healthy revenue growth, expand our operating margin and grow free cash flow.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For Q2&#8217;24, we forecast revenue growth of 16%. This equates to 21% growth on a F&#47;X neutral basis due primarily to price changes in Argentina and the devaluation of the local currency relative to the US dollar. We expect paid net additions to be lower in Q2&#8217;24 vs. Q1&#8217;24 due to typical seasonality. We forecast global ARM to be up year-over-year on a F&#47;X neutral basis in Q2. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For the full year 2024, we expect healthy revenue growth of 13% to 15%, based on </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">F&#47;X rates at the end of Q1&#8217;24</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">4</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. We now expect FY24 operating margin of 25%, based on F&#47;X rates as of January 1, 2024, up from our prior forecast of 24%. As we&#8217;ve noted in the past, while we've launched a F&#47;X risk management program to reduce near term volatility, we don&#8217;t intend to be fully hedged, which is why we guide and manage to a F&#47;X neutral operating margin target. Our goal is to increase our operating margin each year, though the rate of expansion may vary year to year. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">__________________________________</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> Excluding the year over year effect of foreign exchange rate movements and the impact of hedging gains&#47;losses realized as revenues (no hedging gains&#47;losses realized in prior periods). Assumes foreign exchange rates remained constant with foreign exchange rates from each of the corresponding months of the prior-year period.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">2 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">ARM (Average Revenue per Membership) is defined as streaming revenue divided by the average number of streaming paid memberships divided by the number of months in the period. These figures do not include sales taxes or VAT.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">3 </font><font style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Paid Membership Reporting</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As we&#8217;ve noted in previous letters, we&#8217;re focused on revenue and operating margin as our primary financial metrics &#8212; and engagement (i.e. time spent) as our best proxy for customer satisfaction. In our early days, when we had little revenue or profit, membership growth was a strong indicator of our future potential. But now we&#8217;re generating very substantial profit and free cash flow (FCF). We are also developing new revenue streams like advertising and our extra member feature, so memberships are just one component of our growth. In addition, as we&#8217;ve evolved our pricing and plans from a single to multiple tiers with different price points depending on the country, each incremental paid membership has a very different business impact. It&#8217;s why we stopped providing quarterly paid membership guidance in 2023 and, starting next year with our Q1'25 earnings, we will stop reporting quarterly membership numbers and ARM. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We&#8217;ll continue to provide a breakout of revenue by region each quarter and the F&#47;X impact to complement our financials. For guidance, we&#8217;ll add annual revenue guidance on top of what we already provide today&#58; our annual operating margin and free cash flow forecast and forecasts for quarterly revenue, operating income, net income, and EPS. We&#8217;ll also announce major subscriber milestones as we cross them. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Success in streaming starts with engagement. It&#8217;s why we&#8217;ve been providing progressively more information on engagement, starting with our </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Top 10</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">5</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> weekly and most popular lists and more recently our bi-annual </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">report</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">6</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> into viewing on Netflix (which covers &#126;99% of all video watch time on our service). style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Product &#38; Marketing</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">At the root of strong and enduring engagement is fandom. It&#8217;s why our product and marketing are all designed to fuel fandom by helping members discover their next obsession. Our most direct promotional tool is Netflix itself, which has become the go to place for so many people looking for entertainment. Our trailers, for example, generate over 6B impressions every month on Netflix &#8212; more than 40x what they get on YouTube. Across Netflix, upcoming shows and movies received over 25B impressions in March alone, helping to build anticipation for what&#8217;s next. Features like &#8220;Remind Me,&#8221; which notifies members as soon as a title premieres, enable us to turn all that interest into action. And, once titles are released, we believe our personalized recommendations are much more effective at finding audiences than relying on the techniques used in traditional entertainment. It&#8217;s how shows like </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Lupin</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, or films like </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Society of the Snow</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Troll</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> go viral &#8212; reaching much bigger audiences than would ever have been possible in the past.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Beyond Netflix, we use creative marketing to build excitement and fuel fandom. We have bigger and smaller efforts, depending on the genre, potential size of the audience and the conversation we think we can generate. While some campaigns may be more event driven or have significant paid marketing support, social media is a key part of how we drive fandom for our titles. With over 1B followers, we believe that Netflix has one of the largest, most passionate fan bases of any brand in the world on social media. In 2023 alone, our social channels generated over 100B organic impressions. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This hard-to-replicate combination of our reach, recommendations and fandom enables Netflix to push stories into culture in ways that very few can match. The press has dubbed it the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Netflix Effect</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, and it shapes what people search for (</font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Google Year in Review &#8216;23</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">10</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">) and talk about (e.g. </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">One Day</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">11</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">), the music they listen to (e.g. </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">The Greatest Night in Pop</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">12</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, which got </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We Are the World</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> back into the charts again after 40 years), the books they read (e.g. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">14</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">) and how they dress (e.g. </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">The Gentlemen</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">15</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">).</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Cash Flow and Capital Structure</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Net cash generated by operating activities in Q1 was $2.2B and free cash flow</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">16</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> totaled $2.1B (both flat with Q1&#8217;23). During the quarter, we paid down $400M of senior notes with cash on hand and we repurchased 3.6M shares for $2B. We finished the quarter with gross debt of $14B and cash and cash equivalents of $7B. We&#8217;re still forecasting full year 2024 free cash flow of approximately $6B, assuming no material swings in F&#47;X, and cash content spend of up to $17B. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Over the past several years, we have maintained a consistent capital allocation strategy that we believe has served us well&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">2.</font><font gross debt and cash balances equal to approximately 2 months of revenue&#59;</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font and</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">4.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We&#8217;re modestly evolving our capital allocation strategy to better reflect our investment grade status. Going forward, rather than anchoring to $10-$15B of gross debt and minimum cash equivalent to two months of revenue, we&#8217;ll maintain financial policies consistent with a solid investment grade credit rating. In particular, we&#8217;ll continue to prioritize profitable growth by reinvesting in our business, maintain a healthy balance sheet and ample liquidity, and return excess cash (beyond several billion dollars of minimum cash and any used for selective M&#38;A) to shareholders through share repurchases. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As part of this evolution, we&#8217;ve upsized our revolving credit facility from $1B to $3B. This will bolster our access to liquidity, and enable us to improve our cash efficiency, over time. We also expect to refinance our upcoming debt maturities and we don&#8217;t currently have plans to lever up to buy back stock as we value balance sheet flexibility.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter and its attachments include reference to the non-GAAP financial measures of F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin, and free cash flow. Management believes that free cash flow is an important liquidity metric because it measures, during a given period, the amount of cash generated that is available to repay debt obligations, make strategic acquisitions and investments and for certain other activities like stock repurchases. Management believes that F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin allow investors to compare our projected results to our actual results absent year-over-year and intra-year currency fluctuations, respectively, and the impact of restructuring costs. However, these non-GAAP financial measures should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, net income, operating income (profit), operating margin, diluted earnings per share and net cash provided by (used in) operating activities, or other financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. Reconciliation to the GAAP equivalent of these non-GAAP measures are contained in tabular form on the attached unaudited financial statements and in the F&#47;X neutral operating margin disclosure above. We are not able to reconcile forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures because we are unable to predict without unreasonable effort the exact amount or timing of the reconciling items, including property and equipment and change in other assets, and the impact of changes in currency exchange rates. The variability of these items could have a significant impact on our future GAAP financial results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws, including statements regarding our expected results for the fiscal quarter ending June 30, 2024 and fiscal year ending December 31, 2024&#59; adoption and growth of streaming entertainment&#59; growth strategy and outlook&#59; market opportunity&#59; competitive landscape and position&#59; entertainment offerings, including TV shows, movies, games, and live programming&#59; engagement&#59; slate strength&#59; pricing and plans strategy&#59; ad-supported tier and its prospects&#59; ads business&#59; product and marketing strategy&#59; acquisitions&#59; impact of foreign exchange rates&#59; foreign currency exchange hedging program&#59; seasonality&#59; capital allocation strategy&#59; cash balance and spend&#59; stock repurchases&#59; debt refinancings&#59; access to liquidity&#59; cash efficiency&#59; paid net additions&#59; revenue and revenue growth&#59; ARM, operating income, operating margin, net income, earnings per share, and free cash flow&#59; and future reporting of membership information and other data.
